# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've successfully identified and documented all Go source files implementing dashboard JSON model versioning and migration in grafana/grafana. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Findings:

### **Core Migration System** (9 files)
- **`migrate.go`** - Main orchestrator with singleton migrator pattern
- **`migrations.go`** - Schema version registry (v0-42) and migration function map
- **`errors.go`** - Error types for migration tracking
- **`cache.go`** - TTL-based namespace-aware caching for datasources/library elements
- **`datasource_utils.go`** - Datasource reference utilities and index structures
- **`migration_utils.go`** - Shared type conversion and utility functions
- **`frontend_defaults.go`** - Dashboard and panel default application
- **`metrics.go`** - Migration metrics collection
- **`pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/migrator/migrator.go`** - Backend migrator interface

### **Schema Version Migrations** (41 files)
Individual migration files for each schema version (v2 through v42), implementing field-level transformations such as:
- Services filter migration
- Panel minSpan/maxPerRow conversion
- Datasource reference standardization
- Table display mode updates
- Variable and annotation migrations

### **Migration Pipeline Flow:**
1. `Migrate()` function is called with a dashboard and target version
2. Frontend defaults are applied (matching DashboardModel constructor)
3. Panel defaults are applied (matching PanelModel constructor)
4. Unique panel IDs are ensured
5. Schema version migrations run sequentially (v2→v3→...→target)
6. Dashboard is cleaned up for persistence

The complete findings have been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed descriptions of each file's purpose and the key symbols/functions they export.

These functions perform field-level transformations such as:\\n- **v2.go**: Migrates legacy services.filter structure to time and templating properties\\n- **v14.go**: Converts sharedCrosshair boolean to graphTooltip integer\\n- **v17.go**: Converts panel minSpan to maxPerRow\\n- **v27.go**: Migrates constant variables to textbox variables\\n- **v33.go**: Updates datasource references for panels\\n- **v36.go**: Comprehensively migrates datasource references from strings to structured objects with uid, type, and apiVersion\\n- **v38.go**: Migrates table displayMode to cellOptions format\\n- **v42.go**: Migrates hideFrom configuration in field options\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n`apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/datasource_utils.go` provides:\\n- `DatasourceIndex` -
